9a4(mngon pa): ste mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye na yang srog gcod pa spong bas ni tshe ring por 'gyur ro// ma byin par len pa spong bas ni longs spyod chen por 'gyur ro// 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong bas ni chung ma 'gran bla med par
9a5(mngon pa): 'gyur ro// brdzun du smra ba ni spong bas ni skur ba mang bar mi 'gyur ro// phra ma spyang bas ni mdza' bo dang dbye bar mi 'gyur ro// tshig rtsub pa slong bas ni yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra thos par mi 'gyur ro// tshig 'khyal pa spong
9a6(mngon pa): ni tshig mnyam par 'gyur ro// chags sems med pas ni 'dod chags che bar mi 'gyur ro// gnod sems med pas ni zhe sdang che bar mi 'gyur ro// yang dag pa'i lta bas ni gti mug chi bar mi 'gyur ro// sems can
9b1(mngon pa): dmyal bar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po'i tshe'i tshad bskal par len pa 'di mchog yin no// dud 'gro myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni yaM/
9b2(mngon pa): gang gi rnam par smin pas sa srung gi bus su sbyang gi bu nyid dang / rab tu brtan pas rab tu brtan pa nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// yi dgas kyi skye gnas su skye bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas/
9b3(mngon pa): rgyal po gshin rje'i gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di ni mchog yin no// ma'i skye gnas myong ba bar 'gyur pa'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas
9b4(mngon pa): las nus nyid du thob pa 'di mchog yin no// rgyal chen bzhi'i ris myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di mchog yin no// sum
9b5(mngon pa): cu rtsa gsum myong ba'i 'gyur pa'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gling gi rnam par smin pa brgya byin gyis brgya byin nyid thob pa mchog yin no// 'thab bral myong bar 'gyur pa'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin
9b6(mngon pa): bas rab 'thab bral gyis rab 'thab bral nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// dga'i ldan myong por 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas yongs su dga' ldan gyis yongs su dga' ldan nyid thob pa 'di mtshig
10a1(mngon pa): yin no// 'phrul dga' myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gis rnam par smin pas rab sbrul gyis rab sprul nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni
10a2(mngon pa): las gang gi rnam par smin pas dbang byed kyis dbang byed nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams bkres pa dang / skom pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams
10a3(mngon pa): dang tabyang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyas chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod
10a4(mngon pa): do// de yan chad la ni bkres pa dang / sgom pa med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la kha zas 'di lta ste/ 'bras chan dang / zan dang / phye dang / shA dang / rus pa rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub
10a5(mngon pa): kyi ba lang spyod la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras sA lu'i 'bru za'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ni dri za'i zas dang bdud rtsi'i zas za'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba
10a6(mngon pa): bzhin du sum bcu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// de yan chad la ni kham gyi zas med do//
10b1(mngon pa): rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi bdud rtsi ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum bcu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan
10b2(mngon pa): pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang de bzhin no// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bshang pa dang gci ba yod pa bzhin du
10b3(mngon pa): shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams
10b4(mngon pa): la char 'bab mkhas pa dang / char 'bab mi mkhas pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi lci rnams la ni med do//
10b5(mngon pa): de yang chad la yang med do// ji ltar mdzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la lo legs pa dang / mu ge yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyen pa rnams dang / rgyal
10b6(mngon pa): chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la 'jigs pa dang / bde ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi po lang spyod pa rnams la yod do// byang
11a1(mngon pa): gi sgra mi snyan pa gyi mi rnams la ni med do// rgyal tshan bzhi'i lha rnams dang // sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang
11a2(mngon pa): byed pa rnams la yod do// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs gsum pa'o// // mdo la// nyo tshong mdog dang khang pa dang / gding ba dang ni gzhog gos dang // yang ba
11a3(mngon pa): rdul rab skye ba dang / tha dang bgra sA len dang bcu// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor ram/ 'bru 'am/ gser ram dngul nyo tshong bya ba yod pa bzhin du shAr gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams
11a4(mngon pa): lo yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do// de yan chad la yang med do// 'od snyam du/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams ni nor dang 'bru rnams kyis nyo tshong byed do// shar gyi lus
11a5(mngon pa): 'phags pa rnams nai rasmA dang be'u ras rnams kyis so// nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni baljang dang nor bu rnams kyis so zhes zer ba yod do// d+hI 'dzam pra'i gling gi mI rnams kyi mdog stug po dang / dkar po dang / spro bsangs dang /
11a6(mngon pa): mdog skya snar rnam pa bzhi yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams
11b1(mngon pa): kyi mdog ni rnam pa bzhi'o// sngon po dang / ser po dang / dkar po dang / dmar po rnams so// rgyal chen bzhi'i ba rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams
11b2(mngon pa): 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams dang mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta bzhin du tshangs raba'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang
11b3(mngon pa): tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dag pa rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nas skyes
11b4(mngon pa): rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// nam mkha' mtha' yas
11b5(mngon pa): skye mched dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang / ci yang ba'i phyir skye mched dang / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la ni kha dog med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khang pa ched
11b6(mngon pa): du byas pa dang / cheng du byas pa ma yin po dang / khang bzangs dang / sa khong rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang skrod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnam
12a1(mngon pa): kyi khang pa ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'i sa khang ngo // rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang ni ched du byas pa dang tshad du byas pa ma yin pa'o// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyi jis/ ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa
12a2(mngon pa): gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris pa rnams kyis me gzhal med khang rnams ni ched du byas
12a3(mngon pa): pa ma yin no// tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshanges pa'i mdun na 'don pa dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung rnams
12a4(mngon pa): dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mI gladung bya rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang /
12a5(mngon pa): shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyi gzhal mod khang yang ched du byas pa ma yin no// gzugs med pa rnams la ni khang pa med pa'o// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang / bgo ba 'di lta
12a6(mngon pa): ste khal gos dang / sha na'i ras dang / gso ma'i ras dang / zar ma'i ras dang / ras gos dang / zab ngar dang / gau tam pa'i ras dang / D+ha du ko la'i gos dang / a pa ran+ti ka'i gos dang / ras dang / be'u ras yod pa bani/
12b1(mngon pa): shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra ma snyan gyi mi rnams ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos gyon no// ji ltar byung gi sku mi snyan gyis mi rnams dpag bsam shing
12b2(mngon pa): las byung ba'i gos gyon pa bzhin du rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum bcu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dgo' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi
12b3(mngon pa): lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni gos gyon bzhin du skye'o// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams
12b4(mngon pa): dang tshad med pa 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med pa dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras
12b5(mngon pa): bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gyo nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de gos gyon bzhin du skye sa'o// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnam
12b6(mngon pa): kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing ni na rnams pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// bzhag gos rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkri
13a1(mngon pa): po rnams so// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// dpag bsam shing las 'byung ba'i yas ji lta pu 'dod pa de lta
13a2(mngon pa): bu skyes pa 'am/ bud med dag gi sems bskyed ma thag tu de la yal ga 'dud par byed de// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing rnams kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser
13a3(mngon pa): dang dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// bzhag gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnams pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / sem
13a4(mngon pa): rnam dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams sngo// dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji ltar bu 'dod pa de lta bu lha'i bu 'am/ lha'i bu mo dag gi sems bskyed ma thag tu yal ga gdung par byed de/ de'i lag tu 'ong ba'i
13a5(mngon pa): 'gyur ro// rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum bcu rtsa gsum pa dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de
13a6(mngon pa): bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang / bgo ba lci ba dang / yang ba yod pa bzhin
13b1(mngon pa): du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snun pa rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos la srang gcig yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi rmi
13b2(mngon pa): srang phyed do// sum cu r+ya gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi ni srang gi bzhi cha gcig go/ 'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni sbrang gang gi brgyad cha gcig go/ dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni srang gi bcu drug cha gcig go/ 'phrul dga' ba
13b3(mngon pa): rnams kyi sgyum+b+ha cu rtswa gnyis kyi srang gi cha gcig go/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ni srung gi drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cha gcig la med do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi ni gzhal
13b4(mngon pa): du med pa'i gos yin no// tshangs ris kyi kA rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i 'dun na 'dron pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gas
13b5(mngon pa): ba dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung
13b6(mngon pa): ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min lha rnams kyi yang gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no// nye zer gyi yi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig ni rdul phra rab yin no// rdul phra
14a1(mngon pa): rab bdun ni rdul phra ma gcig go// rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zar gyi rdul gcig go/ nye zer gyi rdul bdun lan ri bang gi rdul gcig go/ ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rngun gcig go// lug rdul bdun lan
14a2(mngon pa): glang rdul gcig go// glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go/ so ma bdun la nI a kha gA na gcig go/ a byA ga na gcig la ni ba ti gcig go/ ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go// nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go/ sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la
14a3(mngon pa): ni 'gra 'khru gang ngo // 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kha cig ni khru tshang da ltar brtsis pa'i khru phyed dang bzhi pa'o// kha cig ni khru bzhi pa'o// shar gyi lug 'phags pa rnams ni khru brgyad pa'o// nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni khru bcu drug pa'o// byung
14a4(mngon pa): gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni khru sum cu rtswa gnyis pa'o// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi lus thob pa ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig go/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi phyed do// 'thab bral po rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha
14a5(mngon pa): gsum mo// dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags gcig go// 'phrul dga' ba rnams rgyang grags gcig dang / rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig go// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed rnams kyi ni rgyang grags phyed dang gnyis so// tshangs ris pa
14a6(mngon pa): rnams kyi ni dpag tshang phyeng ngo // tshangs pa mthun na 'don pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gcig go// tshangs pa chen po pa rnams kyi dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis so// 'od srung po rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gnyis so//
14b1(mngon pa): tshad med 'od pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi'o// 'od gsal ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad do// dge chung ba rnams kyi ni dpage tshad bcu drug go// tshad med dge ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad sum cu rtsa gnyis so// dge rgyas pa rnams kyi ni dpag
14b2(mngon pa): tshad drug cu rtsa bzhi'o// sprin med pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga'o// bsod nams skyes pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu'o// 'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi ni dpag tshad lnga brgya'o// 'du shes med pa'i sems can rnams
14b3(mngon pa): kyi yang de dang 'dra'o// mi che ba'i lus thob pa ni dpag tshad stong ngo // mi gdung ba rnams kyi dpag tshad nyis stong ngo // gya nom snang ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi stong ngo // shin tu mthong ba pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad stong ngo / 'og min gyi
14b4(mngon pa): lha rnams kyi lus thob pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad khri drug stong ngo // gzugs med pa rnams la ni bsags pa'i lus med de// nye zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig gi ni rdul phra rab yin no// rdul phra rab bdun la ni rdul phra mo
14b5(mngon pa): gcig go// rdul phra mo bdun la ni nye zer gyi rdul gcig go// nye zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig go// ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go// lug rdul bdun la ni glung rdul gcig go// glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma
14b6(mngon pa): gcig pa// sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga ni gcig go// a ba ga na bdun la ni ba ti ka gcig go// ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go// nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go/ sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la khru gang ngo // 'dzam bu'i gling gi rmi
15a1(mngon pa): rnams kyi kha cig gos khru tshad 'di lta bur brtsis pa'i khru brgyad pa gyon no// kha cig ni khru bcu pa'o// shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams kyi khru nyi shu pa'o// nub bgyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyi ni khru bzhi bcu pa'o// byang gi sgra mi snyan
15a2(mngon pa): pa rnams kyi ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos khru brgyad cu pa gyen gyon no// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyang lus la ci ran pa'i gos gyon no// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ji ltar ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang
15a3(mngon pa): 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dka' ldan ba rnams dang / 'phrul dag pa rnams pa dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang / tshangs ris pa rnams dang / tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen
15a4(mngon pa): po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnas dang / snying med pa rnaMs dang / bsod dmas skyes pa nas dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams
15a5(mngon pa): dang ta mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams dbang po tha dad do// kha cig la ni mo'i dbang po dang /
15a6(mngon pa): kha cig la ni pho'i dbang po yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang / 'thab bral ba
15b1(mngon pa): rnams dang / dge' ldan pa dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mo'i dbang po yang med/ pho'i dbang po yang med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du/ tshangs
15b2(mngon pa): pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa
15b3(mngon pa): rnams dang / nga bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// ji ltar mdzam buni
15b4(mngon pa): gling gi mi rnams la bag ma gtong ba dang / bag ma len pa yod pa bzhin du/ shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba ling spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha
15b5(mngon pa): rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni bag ma gtong
15b6(mngon pa): pa yang med len pa yang med do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams
16a1(mngon pa): dang / dge chung ba dang / tshad med dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba
16a2(mngon pa): rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no// 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs bzhi pa'o// 'jig rten bzhag pa// // bam po gnyis pa/ mdo la/ grang dang tsha dang dus tshigs mtshan mo dang / tha ma
16a3(mngon pa): dang ni rje khol dang / nor dang 'bru dang mngon par zhe na/ bcu tshan yongs su brjod pa yin// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la shin tu grang ba dang / shin tu tsha ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang
16a4(mngon pa): yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la yang med do// de yan chad la yang med do// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la dus tshigs 'di lta ste/ dgun dang / dpyid dang / dbyar yod pa bzhon du sher gyi lus
16a5(mngon pa): 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thal bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /
16a6(mngon pa): gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams lo yang yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dus tshigs med do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang /
16b1(mngon pa): tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba dang / tshad med dag pa rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang /
16b2(mngon pa): gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la mtshan mo dang / nyin mo yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang
16b3(mngon pa): byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha dang / sum cu cu gsum dang rnams dang / 'bras bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do// tshangs ros kyi lha rnams la
16b4(mngon pa): ni mtshan mo yang med/ nyin mo yang med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams
16b5(mngon pa): dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang /
16b6(mngon pa): 'og min gyi rnams la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar mdzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pha dang ma yod pa bzhin drung shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spong pa rnams dang / byang gri sgra mi spyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhin lha rnams dang /
17a1(mngon pa): rba d+ha gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phru / ra bams dang / nan 'al pa du rgya rnams nga yod do// tshangs rab kyi lha rnams lan ma yang mang tha yang mdza// cha
17a2(mngon pa): ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po la rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chud pa rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang /
17a3(mngon pa): dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gyo nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams
17a4(mngon pa): la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la rje bong dang bran yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lug 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do// rgyal
17a5(mngon pa): chen ba'i'i lha rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do// rgyal tshun bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral po rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed
17a6(mngon pa): pa rnams la yid de bzhin na// tshangs rnaMs kyi lha rnams la ni rje bo yang med dran yang med do// ming mi ris pa rnams la ji lte ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'dzin pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / che rdzo
17b1(mngon pa): bod pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba
17b2(mngon pa): rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor dang / 'bru yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang
17b3(mngon pa): spyod pa rnams da la yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni 'bru ni yod ni ri ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni nor ni yod la 'ang ni med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams
17b4(mngon pa): dong / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams nga la yang bzhin na// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni nor yang med 'bru yang med do// tshangs ris kyi lha ji lta
17b5(mngon pa): pa bzhin du tshangs pa mdun ni 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams
17b6(mngon pa): dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams/ gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin
18a1(mngon pa): no Shaji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pa 'am ma 'am/ bu bo'am bu ma 'am/ rje bo 'am/ bran nam/ nor ram/ 'bru la mngon par zhen pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la
18a2(mngon pa): yang yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni ci la'ang mngon par zhen pa med do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni 'bru ma gtogs pa rnams la ni mngon par zhen pa yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa
18a3(mngon pa): rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ba ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la yang mngon par zhen pa med do// tshangs ris pa rnams ji
18a4(mngon pa): lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'a ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams
18a5(mngon pa): dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin
18a6(mngon pa): no// 'jig rten bzhag pa las tshigs lnga pa'o// // mdo la/ zla mtshan 'khrig dang / khu chu dang / tshe bsgyur dang ni chu klung brag/ sa la rdzing bu glang po dang / srungs ma 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam/ ji ltar mdzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bud
18b1(mngon pa): med zla mtshan can dang / sbrum ma dang / bu btsa' ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la yang yod do// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi
18b2(mngon pa): rnams kyi khye'u 'am/ bu mo lo lnga lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin no// lha 'am lha'i bu mo phrag pa 'am phang bar sems can brdzus te skye bar 'gyur to/ de la lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu 'am bu 'amo snyam du sems so// khye'u
18b3(mngon pa): dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so// sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni lo drug lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// 'thab bral rnams kyi ni lo bdun lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// dga' ldan pa rnams
18b4(mngon pa): kyi ni lo brgyad lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// 'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni lo dgu lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi ni khye'u dang bu mo lo bcu lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin du lha
18b5(mngon pa): 'am lha'i bu mo phrag pa'am phang bar brdzus te skye ba'i sems can 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de na lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu 'am bu'i mo snyam du sems so// khye'u dang bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi/
18b6(mngon pa): ma 'am pha'o snyam du sems so// tshangs ris kyi lho rnams ni thog ma nas lus kyi yan lag dang nying lag thams cad rdzogs par skye zhing 'chi ba ni yang de kho na nyid do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don
19a1(mngon pa): ba rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / bod chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'ong ba rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams
19a2(mngon pa): dang bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / grwa nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// gzugs med pa rnams la ni
19a3(mngon pa): yul gyi gzugs med de/ de bas na de dag gi skye ba yang mi mngon no// 'chi lazo ba yang mngon no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling go mi rnams mi tshangs pa spyod pa 'khrig pa'i chos bsten pa ni gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags
19a4(mngon pa): pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyang de bzhin no// thab bral ba rnams ni 'khyud pa tsam gyis gdung ba zhi bar 'gyur ro// dga'
19a5(mngon pa): ldan pa rnams kyis ni lag pa nos bzung ba tsam gyis so// 'phrul dga' ba rnams kyis brkang pa tsam gyis so// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni bltas pa patsam gyis gdung bzhi par 'gyur ro// tshangs ris pa rnams la ni 'dod
19a6(mngon pa): tshigs med do// tshangs ris pa ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshang
19b1(mngon pa): med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams
19b2(mngon pa): dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la khu chu mi gtsang ba 'byung ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyong pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi sbyin gyi mi rnams la
19b3(mngon pa): yang de bzhin no// rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni rlung 'byung ngo // rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ljon pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan
19b4(mngon pa): 'phrul dbang byed kyi yang de bzhin no// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni 'dod chags med do// tshangs ris kyi rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshungs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshang
19b5(mngon pa): med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang /
19b6(mngon pa): mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom pa snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no// sems can dmyal ba'i sems can gyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do//
20a1(mngon pa): dud 'gro'i skye gnas su skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe chud kyi mtha'i skal pa gcig te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// mi rnams kyi nyin bzhag sum cu gang yin pa de ni yi dgas rnams kyi nyin gcig ste/ nyin zhag de sum
20a2(mngon pa): cu la la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ yi dgas rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo khri lnga stong yod do// shar gyi lus 'phags kyi mi rnams
20a3(mngon pa): kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// nub kyi ba lang spyod pa kyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo balnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo stong
20a4(mngon pa): ste khar ma dor 'chi ba med do// ci'i phyir byung gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni bar ma dor 'chi ba med ce na/ de dag la bdag gi ba med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med de// che nges shing khyad par 'gro ba yin pas/ de'i phyir byang gi sgra mi spyan rnams la bar ma
20a5(mngon pa): dor 'chi ba med do// 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la yar skye ba dang / 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams re 'ga' ni tshe dpag tu med par 'gyur la/ re 'ga' ni tshe lo bcu par 'gyur ro// mi rnams kyi ni tshe lo lnga bcu gang yin pa don/ rgyal chen bzhi'i
20a6(mngon pa): lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go// zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar
20b1(mngon pa): brtson lo sa ya phrag dgu yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba yang spos kyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi
20b2(mngon pa): mamatha' ni de lo lta bu ru brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum drug khri nyis stong yod do// mi rnams kyi lo brgya gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi nyin zhag
20b3(mngon pa): gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad ma kyi mtha' ni de lta bu'i brtsis pa'i lha'i lo stong ste/ bar ma der 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba
20b4(mngon pa): phrag gsum dang / sa ya phrag drug yod do// de ni sems can dmyal pa chen po thig nag gi nyin zhag gcig go/ nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig te/ sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi tshe'i tshad
20b5(mngon pa): kyi mtha' ni le de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum phrag bcu gnyis dang / bye ba phrag dgu khri drug stong yod do// mi rnams kyi lo nyis brgya gang
20b6(mngon pa): yin pa de ni 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ 'thab bral ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo nyis stong ste/ bar ma
21a1(mngon pa): dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de'i mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bcu bzhi dang sa ya phrag bzhi yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis
21a2(mngon pa): la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi sems can gyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo nyes stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gcig dang /
21a3(mngon pa): bye ba phrag gsum 'bum drug khri brgyad stong yod do// mi rnams kyi lo bzhi brgya gang yin pa de ni dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i
21a4(mngon pa): tshong ni lo de ltar bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong yod do// bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na la bye ba phrag lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang / los ya phrag drug yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin
21a5(mngon pa): zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi sems can dmyal ba'i ba pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor
21a6(mngon pa): 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bye ba brgyad dang / bye ba phrag so ya gnyis dang / bye ba phrag dgu 'bum po ni khri bzhi stong yod do// mi rnams kyi lo brgyad brgya gang yin pa de ni 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyi nyin zhig gcig go// nyi ma nas/
21b1(mngon pa): sum cu la zla ba gcig go// zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo brgyad stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis ni lo bye ba phrag gnyis brgya sum cu
21b2(mngon pa): dang / lo sa ya phrag bzhi yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen pa'i nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bong chen po'i tshe'i tshad kyi mtha'
21b3(mngon pa): nini lo lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo brgyad stong yod do// bar ma dor chi ba ni yod do// de'i mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag drug cu rtsa drug dang / bye ba phrag sa ya gsum dang / bye ba phrag lnga 'bum lnga khri nyis stong yod de/
21b4(mngon pa): mi rnams kyi lo stong drug brgya gang yin pa de ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi
21b5(mngon pa): mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag dgu brgya nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / lo sa ya phrag drug yod do// de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po che ba'i nyin zhag
21b6(mngon pa): gcig go// nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig/ zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba
22a1(mngon pa): ba'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do// ngo ma'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag lnga brgya dang / lo bye ba phrag bye ba sum cu dang / lo bye ba phrag sa ya brgyad dang / bzhi 'bum dang / lo bye ba phrag khri drug stong yod do// bar
22a2(mngon pa): gyi mdo la/ dgu dang gsum dang bcu bzhi dang ni lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang / nyis brgya dgu brgya rnams ni ma'i grangs kyis lha tsher bshang / de bzhin gcig bcu gnyis gcig dang brgyad drug cu dang / lnga brgya dag ni sems can dmyal ba'i tsher
22a3(mngon pa): bshad do// tshangs pa'i ris kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// sems can dmyal ba chen po rab tu tsha ba'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// tshangs
22a4(mngon pa): pa'i mdun 'don pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bor ma ngor 'chi ba ni yod do// sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med pa'i tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal po gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi kha ni yod do// tshang
22a5(mngon pa): ba chen po ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed dang gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'od chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// tshad med 'od kyi sku rnams kyi tshe'i tshing
22a6(mngon pa): kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'od gsal gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// dge chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal ba bcu / ba
22b1(mngon pa): dor 'chi ba ni yod do// tshad med dge ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gsum cu rtsa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// dge rgyas kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug cu rtsa bzhi ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do//
22b2(mngon pa): sprin med kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga ste/ bar ma ngor 'chi ba ni yod do// bsod nams skyes kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma ngar 'chi ba ni yod do// 'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams
22b3(mngon pa): kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'du shes med pa'i sems can rnams de 'dra'o// mi che ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa stong ste/ bar ma ngor 'chi ba ni yod do// mi gdung ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshang
22b4(mngon pa): kyi mtha' ni bskal ba nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// bla nom snang ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bsgral pa bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// shin tu mthong ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad stong skye
22b5(mngon pa): ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'og min gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched pa'i tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyi khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yang ngo //
22b6(mngon pa): rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'dra
23a1(mngon pa): shes mang 'du shes med min skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do// 'di nas byang phyogs na rin kar po gsum yod do// ri nag po gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri nag pa
23a2(mngon pa): gzhan gsum yod do// ri nag po gzhan gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri'i rgyal po gnas zhes bya ba yod do// 'di ri'i rgyal po gangs kyi byang le phyogs na/ ri'i rgyal po sbam kyi ngad ldang zhes bya ba yod do// ri'i rgyal po spos kyi ngad ltung nas dpag tshad
23a3(mngon pa): bcu'i tshu rol na mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ ma dzes pa zhes kyang bya'o// mtsha chen po chu zhes bya ba de la chur dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do// zheng du dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do// mtha' skor du ni dpag tshad nyis brgya yod de// dbyibs legs
23a4(mngon pa): shing lta na sdug pa badzes pa chu bsil zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang la/ me tog ut+pal dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu dang / pad+ma dkar pos kun tu khebs par 'dug go/ de'i nang nas chu klung chen po bzhi 'di lta ste/ pang+gA dang / sin+d+hu dang / bak+ku dang / si ta dang 'di
23a5(mngon pa): rnams bebi ste/ gang+gA ni shar phyogs nas glang po che'i kha nas 'bab ste/ mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogasu bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu shar phyogs kyi rgyal tsho chen por 'gro'o// sin+d+hu ni lho phyogs nas khyu mchog
23a6(mngon pa): gi kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogasu bskor nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu lho phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o// pak+Sha ni rUb phyogs nas rta'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyog
23b1(mngon pa): su bskor nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu nub phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o// si ta ni byung phyogs nas seng ge'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ krung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu byang phyogs kyi rgya
23b2(mngon pa): mtsho chen por 'gro'o// 'di skad du/ byang phyogs kha dgur 'gyur ba yi// chu mtsho yod de gzhan dag kyang // de na mtsho chen chu zhes bya// tha dad rgyu rnams 'byung nas yod // chu klung gang+gA sin+du pak+Shu dang / si ta dba' rlabs dbu ba'i phreng ba can//
23b3(mngon pa): 'bab cing thams cad gsil ba'i chu yin to// phyogs bzhi kho ra kho ra yug dag nas 'byung // gang+gA shar phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba ste// sin+d+hu lho phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba yin// pak+Shu yang ni nub phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro/ de'i byang phyogs rgya
23b4(mngon pa): mtshor si ta 'gro/ chu klung rab mchog bzhi po 'di dag ni// mchog tu bzang zhing so sor 'beb pa ste/ re re zhing yang lnga brgya khyer nas ni// chu'i rgyun rnams rgya mtsho chen por 'dra zhes kyang bya'o// ri spos kyi ngad ldang de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi
23b5(mngon pa): shu na gser gyi brag byi skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos zhes bya ba yod de/ chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/ mtha' skor du nyis brgya 'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa
23b6(mngon pa): zhig yod de// de'i nang gis sa gzhi yang dbyibs legaso shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsen dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ der yid du mi 'ong ba'i shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung
24a1(mngon pa): na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu gtor ro// de'i kho ra khor yug na gser gyi brag bya skyibs can brgya stong yod do// de dag thams cad kyang legs shing ltan sdug la mdzes pa ste/ de ga dag gi nAngs
24a2(mngon pa): gzhi rnams kyang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa ga sor gyi phyem brdul cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chug btab pa ste/ de dag tu 'ang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag ltung na/ de mim
24a3(mngon pa): yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu 'dor ro// de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zhing dud dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa ba gri bas legs lta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab
24a4(mngon pa): pa zhig yod de/ de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyis rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro// brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad ti bu
24a5(mngon pa): na shing sA la'i rgyal po chen po rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba sA la'i phreng ba rim pa mdun gyis bskor ba zhig yod do// sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de rtsa ba ni 'don bcu bzhi thur du zug go/ sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i rtsa ba ni 'doms
24a6(mngon pa): gsum thur du zug go// gnyis pa'i ni bcu gnyis so// gsum pa'i bcu gcig go// bzhi pa'i ni bcu'o// lnga pa'i ni dgu'o// drug pa ni brgyad do// sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bdun thur du zug go/ sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa

24b3(mngon pa): de ni na mkha' khyab par 'dug go// de'i nang gi sa bzhi yang 'byibs legs shing lta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma brdal cing tsan dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ de yang yid du mi 'ongs pa shing ngam gseg ma 'am gang ci

24b6(mngon pa): dal gyis 'bab ces bya ba chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/ zheng ngu yang dpag tshod lnga bcu ste/ mtha' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya yod pa// dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing chu sbrang rtsi lha bus gang ba/

25b5(mngon pa): cing yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/ de dag gi mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing lta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chu ga sher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod pa shu
25b6(mngon pa): stag ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de 'khor dang bcas pa dgun zla ba bzhi ni brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos gyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do// dpyid zla ba bzhi ni shing sA li'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing
26a1(mngon pa): 'khod do// dbyar zla ba bzhi ni rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do// gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni glang po che brgyad stong po

26a3(mngon pa): gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing sA la'i rgyal po pa rab tu brtan pa'i nang na du 'gro ba na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal po'i tshul gyis 'gro'o// res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha dang lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul

26a5(mngon pa): tu brtan pa'i nang na shing gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe glang po che rgyas stong po 'di dag kyang 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa bsrung ba dang / sba ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir shing sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun po dag gi nang na
26a6(mngon pa): kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do// shing sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de ni dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod de// gnyis pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dog kyang kha nang du lte sa'o// gsum pa'i nang du 'dug pa gang
26b1(mngon pa): yin pa de dag kyang nang kha nang du lta'o// bzhi pa'i nang du 'dug pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// la pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// drug pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o// bdun pa'i nang na
26b2(mngon pa): 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do// gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa nas rdzing bu dral gyis 'bab par 'gra na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal bI'i tshul gyis 'gro'o//
26b3(mngon pa): res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha 'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che de dag thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo bo 'am/ rgyab tu

26b5(mngon pa): lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de bsro ba dang / sde ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir rdzing bu dal gyi 'bab kyis/ mtha' kho ra khor yug nas bskur te khA nang du bltas shing 'khod do// gong gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing
